 dilli kii ore se irfan, kaul or nadeem ne ek-ek safalataa hasil kii

 irfan pathan (naabad 23) or morne morkal (19) ne ravi rampal dwaara phenk gaye 19wein over main 15 ran liye

 irfan ne 11 gedon par do chauke or do chakke lagaae
 Umesh Yadav returned unbeaten on four runs

 yahaan tak ki film ke nirdesan se bhi jitu aroda ke alaava khud gurmeet ram rahim jude rahe hai

 haa, lekin un logon ko yah film zarur baba ram rahim or deraa sachcha sauda kaa prachaar lagegi, jo unke shishy nahin hai
 The social evils depicted in the film are a bitter reality in the current situation
 filmkaaron or film ke jaankaron ko ho saktaa he film takneekee taur par or baaki vibhaagon ko dekhte hue mazaaq lage, lekin film main diya gaya sandesh sanjeeda or thos he
 The film narrates the life of Sant Ram Rahim to a large extent
 baba film main logon ko drugs or sharaab jaisi lat se dur kar apana anuyaayi banaate hai, jiske kaaran drug or sharaab mafia baba ke dushman ban jate hai

 film main baba ram rahim ke saath flora saini or jai shri bhi hai

 agar aap sanni deol, ajay devgan, rajnikant or salmaan khan ke ection ko pachaa sakate hai to sant ram rahim kaa ection kyon nahin

 is baat main koi do raay nahin ki baba abhinay main kachche hai, lekin unka canvikshan, yani apane kirdaar par unka drudh vishwaas dekhne laayak he

 ram rahim ke abhinay or dance kii kamazoriyon ko fatafat badalte seen se chhipaane kii koshish kii gai he, yani gaanon kii editing acchhee he
 Speaking of flaws, the quality of special effects is quite poor

 masalan, raktadan, veshyavriti se ladakiyon ko baahar nikaalnaa, sharaab, drug, yahaan tak ki global warming ke khilaaf muhim

 Father Pedvenkappa Raju and mother Ishwaramma named Satyanarayana Raju

 1954:puttaparthi main 12 bistaron vaale aspataal kii sthapana kii

 1972:shri satya sai central trust kii sthapana kii
 It is the Paramarth Trust which undertakes social welfare projects
 1976:bangaloru main aspataal kii sthapana kii

 1981:shri satya sai institute for hair larning kii sthapana kii, jo ki dimd vishvavidhyalay he
 1991: Established the 220-bed Sathya Sai Institute for Higher Medical Sciences
 1993:prasanti nilayam main baba ke shayankaksh main chaar log ghus aae, jinhen maar daalaa gaya
 This matter remains a puzzle so far
 1995:anantpur peyajal pariyojna kii shuruyaat kii
 1999: The Department of Posts and Telegrams issued a stamp for their efforts to solve drinking water problems
 2000:apane amrit mahotsav kaaryakramon ke tahat chaitanya jyoti vishwa dharm sangrahalay kaa udghaatan kiya
 2001: Started Medak and Mahbubnagar water projects
 bangaloru ke whitefield main 333 bistaron vaale aspataal kii sthapana kii
 Inaugurated the digital radio network Radio Sai Global Harmony
 2002:chennai jal pariyojna shuru kii
 2007: Started East and West Godavari water projects

 aise main date aadhaarit utpaada equity kii tulana main zyada surakshit maane jate hai
 On Wednesday, the Cabinet approved the country's first corporate bond-based ETF "bharat Bond ETF"
 bharat bond desh kaa pehla bond itief hoga
 Earlier, only equity-based etfs were traded in the country
 vitt mantri nirmala sitaraman ke mutabik isse sarkari companiyon or sansthaaon ko fund kaa atirikt strot milegaa
 Bond trades issued by government entities can be made under Bharat Bond ETF
 itief kii unit kaa mulya 1000 rupye hoga, jisase chote niveshak isamen zyada se zyada hissedari le sake
 There are two periods of maturity under this ETF, the first three years and the second eight years

 yah pehla aisa mauka hoga jab aam janata bond market se jud sakegi ’’ abhi desh main bond bazaar se jude utpaada bahut lokapriy nahin hai

 How to expect returns in bond etfs? Bond etfs can give good returns compared to traditional investment channels such as bank deposits etc
 haalanki 3 saal kii paripakvata vaale itief mahangaai kii dar ko maat de paaenge yah kahana mushkil he
 The rate of government bonds will form the basis of returns of these etfs

 That is, the risk is limited
 lekin is utpaada main taralata ek mushkil ho sakati he
